<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парализовать.html>парализова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">paralizovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to paralyze, to palsy</li>
<li>to petrify</li>
<li>to paralyze
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забастовка.html>забасто́вка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:парализовать.html>парализова́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:связь.html>связь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zabastóvka <b>paralizovála</b> svjazʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the strike paralyzed communications</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***параллель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:параллель.html>паралле́ль</a> (15448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параллель.html>паралле́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">parallélʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параллель.html>паралле́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параллель.html>паралле́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параллель.html>паралле́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geometry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> parallel (line)</li>
<li>parallel (line of latitude)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>города́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:находиться.html>нахо́дятся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:параллель.html>паралле́ли</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éti gorodá naxódjatsja na odnój <b>paralléli</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">These towns have the same latitude.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>parallel (line of reasoning similar to another one)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преподаватель.html>преподава́тель</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:провести.html>провёл</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:параллель.html>паралле́ль</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:между.html>ме́жду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тими</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:факт.html>фа́ктами</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Prepodavátelʹ provjól <b>parallélʹ</b> méždu étimi fáktami.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The teacher established similarity between these facts.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***параша.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ша</a> (13322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ша</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">paráša</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ши</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ш</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>close-stool in a prison</li>
<li>bullshit, nonsense, untrue rumors</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The place near <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ша</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paráša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is considered the least prestigious in Russian prison cells, which are often shared by many inmates. It is often reserved to the so called <i><a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>петухи́</a></i>, passive homosexuals, the lowest standing caste in the Russian prison caste system. The word is therefore associated with something having very low quality. It can also be used in expressions such as <i><a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>Твоё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>место</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:параша.html>пара́ши</a></i>, 'Your place is at the close-stool', which is considered utterly insulting.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:парить.html>пари</a> (11736)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">pari</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">second-person singular imperative imperfective of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парить.html>пари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:париться.html>па́рившийся</a> (17055)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:парикмахер.html>парикма́хер</a> (7758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Perückenmacher</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wig-maker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">perruque</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wig</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Macher</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">maker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парикмахер.html>парикма́хер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">parikmáxer</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парикмахер.html>парикма́хера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парикмахер.html>парикма́херы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парикмахер.html>парикма́херов</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:парилка.html>пари́лка</a> (27206)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парить.html>па́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">páritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with stress shift.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pariti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="переносное значение">перен.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="книжное">книжн.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="устаревшее">устар.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:стремиться.html>стреми́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́кому</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:находиться.html>находи́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:область.html>о́бласти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возвышенный.html>возвы́шенных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идея.html>иде́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предмет.html>предме́тов</a>; <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="ироничное">ирон.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:мечтать.html>мечта́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:предаваться.html>предава́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фантазия.html>фанта́зиям</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

***парк.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>парк</a> (1758)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Park</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">park</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">parc</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>парк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">park</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>па́рка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>па́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>па́рков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>park <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for recreation</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:парк.html>па́рк</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знаменитый.html>знамени́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:статуя.html>ста́туями</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Étot <b>párk</b> znamenít svoími státujami.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">This <b>park</b> is famous for its statues.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>yard, depot</li>
<li>fleet, stock</li>
<li>depot</li></ol>
